text-align: center;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-kDJh58ZseD0/VCjsPNEcsfI/AAAAAAAAwgA/0tAhr7CUxSQ/s1600/sky_uuma1.gif\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"410\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-kDJh58ZseD0/VCjsPNEcsfI/AAAAAAAAwgA/0tAhr7CUxSQ/s1600/sky_uuma1.gif\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-size: large;\"><b><span style=\"color: red;\">SAPTARISHIS</span>-- <span style=\"color: blue;\">DRUV</span> --<span style=\"color: purple;\"> THE POLE STAR</span>-- NORTH STAR -- THE GREAT DIPPER --<span style=\"color: magenta;\">URSA MAJOR.</span></b></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-size: large;\"><b><span style=\"color: magenta;\"><br /></span></b></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-T-yb87-KPwA/TlEqV-JSTII/AAAAAAAAFm8/1oi5hWUlgUY/s1600/vgh.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-T-yb87-KPwA/TlEqV-JSTII/AAAAAAAAFm8/1oi5hWUlgUY/s1600/vgh.png\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\">King Uttanapada had two wives. The older one was Suniti and the younger was Suruchi. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\">Elder Queen Suniti was kind and graceful, and she had a son by the name of Druv.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-F8_oRFKHHno/TlDngW7CiyI/AAAAAAAAFmg/kSfV54zPLio/s1600/YH.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-F8_oRFKHHno/TlDngW7CiyI/AAAAAAAAFmg/kSfV54zPLio/s1600/YH.png\" width=\"187\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\">The younger queen Suruchi was very beautiful, but vain.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>She had a son by the name of Uttama. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\">Suruchi was afraid Prince Druv would become king as per royal tradition.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\">The King was under the spell of the dazzling beauty Suruchi. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\">Once Druv saw his younger brother Uttam sitting on their father\u2019s lap. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Little Druv asked his father to <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>give him a seat on his lap too. Pretty soon the king was sitting with both boys on his lap. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\">This sight infuriated Suruchi who screamed and <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>made Druv get down from the king\u2019s lap.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-vVATcScqEvQ/TlEMs2bZ9AI/AAAAAAAAFm4/-niJ6_bgOzo/s1600/imagesCAL9626A.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"284\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-vVATcScqEvQ/TlEMs2bZ9AI/AAAAAAAAFm4/-niJ6_bgOzo/s1600/imagesCAL9626A.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\">The humiliated little child ran to Suneeti and fighting back tears , recounted what had transpired. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\">He asked his mother \u201c Is anybody more important and stronger&nbsp;than the king?\u201d<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\">Suneeti consoled little Druv by telling him \u201c Lord Vishnu is more powerful\u201d<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\">Druv asked \u201c Where does he live?\u201d<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\">Suniti said \u201c<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>In those mountains \u201d<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\">At night Druv slipped away into the darkness , and walked towards the mountains.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-6Ym87dBdHuY/TlDnnioqZ0I/AAAAAAAAFmk/g8gQzVmfJ_g/s1600/untitledCGH.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"300\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-6Ym87dBdHuY/TlDnnioqZ0I/AAAAAAAAFmk/g8gQzVmfJ_g/s1600/untitledCGH.png\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\">He met Sage Narada and asked for advise. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Narad muni dissuaded Druv from undertaking such a difficult task.&nbsp;<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-QdQ_5hZ4CkA/TlEMc522OzI/AAAAAAAAFmw/OS3Rzh0O1j8/s1600/imagesCA9ETHD7.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-QdQ_5hZ4CkA/TlEMc522OzI/AAAAAAAAFmw/OS3Rzh0O1j8/s1600/imagesCA9ETHD7.jpg\" width=\"268\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\">Narada told Druv: \"You are young,\u2026even great sages have not achieved the Almighty...\" <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-j4nTAfwNySM/TlDmKdi9_xI/AAAAAAAAFmY/0adNja8GrI4/s1600/imagesCA9IROX4.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-j4nTAfwNySM/TlDmKdi9_xI/AAAAAAAAFmY/0adNja8GrI4/s1600/imagesCA9IROX4.jpg\" width=\"278\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\">Seeing Dhruv adamant, sage Narada taught Druv the technique of prayer and asked him to chant the supreme mantra: \"Om Namo Bhagavate Vaasudevaaya\". <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-muhr1bOfNj4/TlDnt6HjQwI/AAAAAAAAFmo/cRgcZYtjNWU/s1600/imagesCA8LDZG6.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-muhr1bOfNj4/TlDnt6HjQwI/AAAAAAAAFmo/cRgcZYtjNWU/s1600/imagesCA8LDZG6.jpg\" width=\"275\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\">Narada told him to sit where he was and meditate. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Druv started meditating ,&nbsp;drinking only<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>water from the Yamuna river. </span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-hW_yL0LRovg/TlEMRxcHn1I/AAAAAAAAFms/f6dGXkbvfvM/s1600/imagesCAEWNNO0.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-hW_yL0LRovg/TlEMRxcHn1I/AAAAAAAAFms/f6dGXkbvfvM/s1600/imagesCAEWNNO0.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\">He released so much energy that the Saptarishis <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>( 7 sages ) got disturbed from their meditation. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-AeGC8YDUEBw/TlDmAyy7CRI/AAAAAAAAFmQ/mHwBzQSw9vI/s1600/imagesCA0PTD2M.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"398\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-AeGC8YDUEBw/TlDmAyy7CRI/AAAAAAAAFmQ/mHwBzQSw9vI/s1600/imagesCA0PTD2M.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n</div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\">They discussed among themselves and came to the unanimous conclusion that only a god can create such tremendous energy. They decided to investigate and were very surprised to see a small child in deep meditation. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\">The King of Gods Indra got worried . With such energy even his own throne was in danger of getting usurped. He tried his best to disturb the little boy. The seven sages protected the boy . <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Druv could not be disturbed, so great was his concentration. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\">Ultimately Vishnu came and stood in front of the little boy. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>The boy opened his eyes, and smiled. The Lord knew that Druv had started his penance, only because he had wanted to sit in his father\u2019s lap, and was not allowed to.&nbsp;<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-wvl_rufUCks/TlDmFSgIpyI/AAAAAAAAFmU/UaMXAHOMXX8/s1600/imagesCACCZY7T.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-wvl_rufUCks/TlDmFSgIpyI/AAAAAAAAFmU/UaMXAHOMXX8/s1600/imagesCACCZY7T.jpg\" width=\"283\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\"></span>Vishnu placed Dhruv on his Divine father\u2019s lap as the Pole Star, also known as the North Star.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-NNgVx5n1WdA/TlDmP4uanuI/AAAAAAAAFmc/PTuoeDpgQUs/s1600/imagesCARUHSMD.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-NNgVx5n1WdA/TlDmP4uanuI/AAAAAAAAFmc/PTuoeDpgQUs/s1600/imagesCARUHSMD.jpg\" width=\"276\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\">Vishnu placed the seven sages to protect him, with Kratu and Pulaha in immediate charge.</span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\">THUS A SMALL BOY WHO WAS THROWN OUT IN A DISGRACEFUL MANNER FROM THE KING'S LAP,&nbsp; WAS NOW PERMANENTLY ENSCONSED IN THE LAP OF THE SUPREME COSMIC LORD.</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-cIdS9RbBUtQ/TlDlvc0PuYI/AAAAAAAAFmI/w_BTosbBoUM/s1600/untitledabc.jpg.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"185\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-cIdS9RbBUtQ/TlDlvc0PuYI/AAAAAAAAFmI/w_BTosbBoUM/s1600/untitledabc.jpg.png\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\">In Hindu astronomy the seven stars of the Saptarshi Mandal or Big Dipper or Ursa Major are named as<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-wuvSi6Xc2YQ/TlDlIiHQGzI/AAAAAAAAFl8/l5LDTW2iExY/s1600/imagesCA2W3RZ5.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><strong><em>Indian Name/<span style=\"mso-tab-count: 1;\">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Bayer/<span style=\"mso-tab-count: 1;\">&nbsp; </span>Western name<o:p></o:p></em></strong></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><em><span style=\"color: blue;\">Kratu/\u03b1 /Dubhe</span></em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><em><span style=\"color: blue;\">Pulaha/\u03b2 /Merak</span></em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><em><span style=\"color: blue;\">Atri/\u03b4 /Megrez</span></em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; , &quot;serif&quot;;\">But the credit for discovery of Polaris and Great bear constellation of 7 stars is given to Greeko Ptolemy in 140 AD. </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\">The architect Maharshi sage of Bhrigu clan, (Imhotep) sailed from Kerala to create&nbsp;the Sphinx on a sink hole in Egypt (using the Pole star) 6000 years ago.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; WHEN IT IS DIES IT FLOATS DOWN STREAM..</span><br /><br />All of the stars \u201cappear\u201d to rotate in the sky due to the fact that the earth is rotating on its axis. Because the north pole is tilted towards Polaris, all of the stars in this part of the sky appear to rotate around this fixed point.<br /><br />NOW\u2014<br /><br /><span style=\"color: purple;\">WHEN THE FATHER DIES THE SON WALKS AROUND THE PYRE ( BEFORE LIGHTING ) ANTI-CLOCKWISE..</span><br />When the father dies , the eldest son is in the lead bare chested with untied kudumi .<br /><br />The eldest son carries a pot of water on his left shoulder, using his right hand to hold the ganges water pot in place. He has to circumambulate (or go around) the body three times in an anti-clockwise direction, from left to right. The younger sons follow behind him.<br /><br /><br />When the eldest son circumambulates the body, the priest makes a hole in the pot so as to allow water to spout wetting his untied kudumi.<br /><br />Water holds memory.<br /><br />Each time he circumambulates ( 3 times ) , a new hole is made.<br /><br />In the first circumambulation, the water that flows facilitates the departure of the soul from this world. During the second circumambulation, the water that flows is to purify the atmosphere. During the third circumambulation, the water that flows is to lead the soul to heaven.<br /><br /><br />After the third circumambulation, the son faces north and throws the pot over the shoulder southwards, over his back. ..<br /><br /><br />The elder son squeezes a few drops from his wet untied kudumi into his dead father\u2019s mouth. Remember his father had once done it , long ago, on the 16th day of his birth.<br /><br />This is like a relay baton passing on. After this he is not to look back . The symbolizes the break of the father\u2019s soul , with planet earth.<br /><br />Capt ajit vadakayil<br />..</div>\n</div>\n</li>\n</ol>\n</div>\n</span></div>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both;
